<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="center"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">ADVANCED SEMICONDUCTOR ENGINEERING, INC. REPORTS UNAUDITED CONSOLIDATED FINANCIAL RESULTS FOR THE THIRD QUARTER OF 2010</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">Taipei, Taiwan, R.O.C., October 29, 2010 &#8211; Advanced Semiconductor Engineering, Inc. (TAIEX: 2311, NYSE: ASX) (&#8220;We&#8221;, &#8220;ASE&#8221;, or the &#8220;Company&#8221;), the world&#8217;s largest independent provider of IC packaging and testing services, today reported unaudited net revenue<font style="FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: text-top"><a href="#ref.ID0E4EAC">1</a></font> of NT$51,489 million for the third quarter of 2010 (3Q10), up by 104% year-over-year and up by 11% sequentially.&#160;&#160;Net income for the quarter totaled NT$5,460 million, up from a net income of NT$3,187 million in 3Q09 and NT$4,613 million in 2Q10.&#160;&#160;Diluted earnings per share for the quarter was NT$0.91 (or US$0.143 per ADS), compared to diluted earnings per share of NT$<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">0.</font>56 for 3Q09
 and NT$<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">0.</font>76 for 2Q10<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">.</font></font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>
</div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">To aid investors in understanding the significance of the Company's successful tender offer for 98.9% of the outstanding common shares of Universal Scientific Industrial Co., Ltd. ("USI") in the second and third quarter of 2010, this earnings release includes (i) the Company's pro forma and actual financial results both reflecting the consolidation of USI, and (ii) consolidated financial results for USI.&#160;&#160;USI's financial results are reflected in the Company's actual financial results for the first quarter beginning in February 2010 and for the second and third quarter of 2010.&#160;&#160;The pro forma financial results reflect the completion of the USI tender offer as if it had occurred on January 1, 2009<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">.</font>&#160;&#160;The presentation of the financial results for USI and the Compa
ny as described above are for purposes of this earnings release only.</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt"><br>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">RESULTS OF OPERATIONS</font></div>

</div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; TEXT-DECORATION: underline">IC Packaging Services</font><font style="FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: text-top"><a href="#ref.ID0EGGAG">3</a></font></font></div>

<div>

</td>
</tr></table>
</div>

<div>

</td>
</tr></table>
</div>

<div>
<table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" id="list" width="100%" style="FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: times new roman">

<div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">Gross margin for our IC packaging operations during the quarter was 22%, up by 1 percentage point from the same quarter last year and the same as the previous quarter<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">.</font></font></div>
</td>
</tr></table>
</div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-STYLE: italic; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">About ASE, Inc.</font></div>

<div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-STYLE: italic; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">ASE<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">,</font> Inc. is the world's largest independent provider of IC packaging services and testing services, including front-end engineering testing, wafer probing and final testing services.&#160;&#160;ASE, Inc.&#8217;s international customer base of more than 200 customers includes such leading names as ATI Technologies Inc., MediaTek Inc., Broadcom Corporation, NVIDIA Corporation, NXP Semiconductors, Qualcomm Incorporated, Renesas Electronics Corporation, RF Micro Devices Inc. and STMicroelectronics N.V.&#160;&#160;With advanced technological capabilities and a global presence spanning Taiwan, China, Korea, Japan, Singapore, Malaysia and the United States, ASE<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">,</font> Inc. has established a reputation for reliable, high quali
ty products and services.&#160;&#160;For more information, visit our website at http://www.aseglobal.com<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-FAMILY: Arial">.</font></font></div>
